#To try and use some of the many historical families HIP added for Italy that held baronies and not full counties. Given baronies weren't on the map in CK2 it was a lot easier to actually make the proper baronies for the various families and CK2 actually stored title history for baronies. Given baronies are pointless in CK3 and store no title data it's better to just give a family a full title that's just held by a King anyway
